1516    private Builder<List<Tuple>> getTupleListBuilder() {
1517      return proto == RedisProtocol.RESP3 ? BuilderFactory.TUPLE_LIST_RESP3 : BuilderFactory.TUPLE_LIST;
1518    }
1519    private Builder<Set<Tuple>> getTupleSetBuilder() {
1520      return proto == RedisProtocol.RESP3 ? BuilderFactory.TUPLE_ZSET_RESP3 : BuilderFactory.TUPLE_ZSET;
1521    }

1878    public final CommandObject<String> xgroupCreate(byte[] key, byte[] groupName, byte[] id, boolean makeStream) {

2024    public final CommandObject<List<Map.Entry<String, List<StreamEntry>>>> xread(
2025        XReadParams xReadParams, Map<String, StreamEntryID> streams) {
2026      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(XREAD).addParams(xReadParams).add(STREAMS);
2027      Set<Map.Entry<String, StreamEntryID>> entrySet = streams.entrySet();
2028      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.key(entry.getKey()));
2029      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.add(entry.getValue()));
2030      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STREAM_READ_RESPONSE);
2031    }
2032    public final CommandObject<List<Map.Entry<String, List<StreamEntry>>>> xreadGroup(
2033        String groupName, String consumer, XReadGroupParams xReadGroupParams,
2034        Map<String, StreamEntryID> streams) {
2035      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(XREADGROUP)
2036          .add(GROUP).add(groupName).add(consumer)
2037          .addParams(xReadGroupParams).add(STREAMS);
2038      Set<Map.Entry<String, StreamEntryID>> entrySet = streams.entrySet();
2039      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.key(entry.getKey()));
2040      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.add(entry.getValue()));
2041      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STREAM_READ_RESPONSE);
2042    }
2043    public final CommandObject<List<byte[]>> xread(XReadParams xReadParams, Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]>... streams) {
2044      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(XREAD).addParams(xReadParams).add(STREAMS);
2045      for (Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]> entry : streams) {
2046        args.key(entry.getKey());
2047      }
2048      for (Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]> entry : streams) {
2049        args.add(entry.getValue());
2050      }
2051      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.BINARY_LIST);
2052    }

2424    private boolean isRoundRobinSearchCommand() {
2425      if (broadcastAndRoundRobinConfig == null) {
2426        return true;
2427      } else if (broadcastAndRoundRobinConfig.getRediSearchModeInCluster() == JedisBroadcastAndRoundRobinConfig.RediSearchMode.LIGHT) {
2428        return false;
2429      }
2430      return true;
2431    }
2432    private CommandArguments checkAndRoundRobinSearchCommand(CommandArguments commandArguments, String indexName) {
2433      return isRoundRobinSearchCommand() ? commandArguments.add(indexName) : commandArguments.key(indexName);
2434    }
2435    private CommandArguments checkAndRoundRobinSearchCommand(CommandArguments commandArguments, byte[] indexName) {
2436      return isRoundRobinSearchCommand() ? commandArguments.add(indexName) : commandArguments.key(indexName);
2437    }
2438    private <T> CommandObject<T> directSearchCommand(CommandObject<T> object, String indexName) {
2439      object.getArguments().processKey(indexName);
2440      return object;
2441    }
2442    public final CommandObject<String> ftCreate(String indexName, IndexOptions indexOptions, Schema schema) {
2443      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(SearchCommand.CREATE).add(indexName)
2444          .addParams(indexOptions).add(SearchKeyword.SCHEMA);
2445      schema.fields.forEach(field -> args.addParams(field));
2446      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STRING);
2447    }

3226    private JsonObjectMapper getJsonObjectMapper() {
3227      JsonObjectMapper localRef = this.jsonObjectMapper;
3228      if (Objects.isNull(localRef)) {
3229        synchronized (this) {
3230          localRef = this.jsonObjectMapper;
3231          if (Objects.isNull(localRef)) {
3232            this.jsonObjectMapper = localRef = new DefaultGsonObjectMapper();
3233          }
3234        }
3235      }
3236      return localRef;
3237    }
3238    public void setJsonObjectMapper(JsonObjectMapper jsonObjectMapper) {
3239      this.jsonObjectMapper = jsonObjectMapper;
3240    }

3242      if (dialect == 0) throw new IllegalArgumentException("DIALECT=0 cannot be set.");
3243      this.searchDialect.set(dialect);

3245    private class SearchProfileResponseBuilder<T> extends Builder<Map.Entry<T, Map<String, Object>>> {
3246      private final Builder<T> replyBuilder;
3247      public SearchProfileResponseBuilder(Builder<T> replyBuilder) {
3248        this.replyBuilder = replyBuilder;
3249      }
3250      @Override
3251      public Map.Entry<T, Map<String, Object>> build(Object data) {
3252        List<Object> list = (List<Object>) data;
3253        return KeyValue.of(replyBuilder.build(list.get(0)),
3254            SearchBuilderFactory.SEARCH_PROFILE_PROFILE.build(list.get(1)));
3255      }
3256    }
3257    private class JsonObjectBuilder<T> extends Builder<T> {
3258      private final Class<T> clazz;
3259      public JsonObjectBuilder(Class<T> clazz) {
3260        this.clazz = clazz;
3261      }
3262      @Override
3263      public T build(Object data) {
3264        return getJsonObjectMapper().fromJson(BuilderFactory.STRING.build(data), clazz);
3265      }
3266    }
3267    private class JsonObjectListBuilder<T> extends Builder<List<T>> {
3268      private final Class<T> clazz;
3269      public JsonObjectListBuilder(Class<T> clazz) {
3270        this.clazz = clazz;
3271      }
3272      @Override
3273      public List<T> build(Object data) {
3274        if (data == null) {
3275          return null;
3276        }
3277        List<String> list = BuilderFactory.STRING_LIST.build(data);
3278        return list.stream().map(s -> getJsonObjectMapper().fromJson(s, clazz)).collect(Collectors.toList());
3279      }
3280    }
3281    private static final Builder<Map.Entry<Long, byte[]>> BLOOM_SCANDUMP_RESPONSE = new Builder<Map.Entry<Long, byte[]>>() {

3283      public Map.Entry<Long, byte[]> build(Object data) {
3284        List<Object> list = (List<Object>) data;
3285        return new KeyValue<>(BuilderFactory.LONG.build(list.get(0)), BuilderFactory.BINARY.build(list.get(1)));

3288    private CommandArguments addFlatArgs(CommandArguments args, long... values) {
3289      for (long value : values) {
3290        args.add(value);
3291      }
3292      return args;
3293    }
3294    private CommandArguments addFlatArgs(CommandArguments args, double... values) {
3295      for (double value : values) {
3296        args.add(value);
3297      }
3298      return args;
3299    }
3300    private CommandArguments addFlatKeyValueArgs(CommandArguments args, String... keyvalues) {
3301      for (int i = 0; i < keyvalues.length; i += 2) {
3302        args.key(keyvalues[i]).add(keyvalues[i + 1]);
3303      }
3304      return args;
3305    }
3306    private CommandArguments addFlatKeyValueArgs(CommandArguments args, byte[]... keyvalues) {
3307      for (int i = 0; i < keyvalues.length; i += 2) {
3308        args.key(keyvalues[i]).add(keyvalues[i + 1]);
3309      }
3310      return args;
3311    }
3312    private CommandArguments addFlatMapArgs(CommandArguments args, Map<?, ?> map) {
3313      for (Map.Entry<? extends Object, ? extends Object> entry : map.entrySet()) {
3314        args.add(entry.getKey());
3315        args.add(entry.getValue());
3316      }
3317      return args;
3318    }
3319    private CommandArguments addSortedSetFlatMapArgs(CommandArguments args, Map<?, Double> map) {
3320      for (Map.Entry<? extends Object, Double> entry : map.entrySet()) {
3321        args.add(entry.getValue());
3322        args.add(entry.getKey());
3323      }
3324      return args;
3325    }
3326    private CommandArguments addGeoCoordinateFlatMapArgs(CommandArguments args, Map<?, GeoCoordinate> map) {
3327      for (Map.Entry<? extends Object, GeoCoordinate> entry : map.entrySet()) {
3328        GeoCoordinate ord = entry.getValue();
3329        args.add(ord.getLongitude());
3330        args.add(ord.getLatitude());
3331        args.add(entry.getKey());
3332      }
3333      return args;
3334    }

1516    private Builder<List<Tuple>> getTupleListBuilder() {
1517      return proto == RedisProtocol.RESP3 ? BuilderFactory.TUPLE_LIST_RESP3 : BuilderFactory.TUPLE_LIST;
1518    }
1519    private Builder<Set<Tuple>> getTupleSetBuilder() {
1520      return proto == RedisProtocol.RESP3 ? BuilderFactory.TUPLE_ZSET_RESP3 : BuilderFactory.TUPLE_ZSET;
1521    }

2024    public final CommandObject<List<Map.Entry<String, List<StreamEntry>>>> xread(
2025        XReadParams xReadParams, Map<String, StreamEntryID> streams) {
2026      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(XREAD).addParams(xReadParams).add(STREAMS);
2027      Set<Map.Entry<String, StreamEntryID>> entrySet = streams.entrySet();
2028      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.key(entry.getKey()));
2029      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.add(entry.getValue()));
2030      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STREAM_READ_RESPONSE);
2031    }

2033        String groupName, String consumer, XReadGroupParams xReadGroupParams,

2036          .add(GROUP).add(groupName).add(consumer)
2037          .addParams(xReadGroupParams).add(STREAMS);
2038      Set<Map.Entry<String, StreamEntryID>> entrySet = streams.entrySet();
2039      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.key(entry.getKey()));
2040      entrySet.forEach(entry -> args.add(entry.getValue()));
2041      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STREAM_READ_RESPONSE);
2042    }
2043    public final CommandObject<List<byte[]>> xread(XReadParams xReadParams, Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]>... streams) {
2044      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(XREAD).addParams(xReadParams).add(STREAMS);
2045      for (Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]> entry : streams) {
2046        args.key(entry.getKey());
2047      }
2048      for (Map.Entry<byte[], byte[]> entry : streams) {
2049        args.add(entry.getValue());
2050      }
2051      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.BINARY_LIST);
2052    }

2424    private boolean isRoundRobinSearchCommand() {
2425      if (broadcastAndRoundRobinConfig == null) {
2426        return true;
2427      } else if (broadcastAndRoundRobinConfig.getRediSearchModeInCluster() == JedisBroadcastAndRoundRobinConfig.RediSearchMode.LIGHT) {
2428        return false;
2429      }
2430      return true;
2431    }
2432    private CommandArguments checkAndRoundRobinSearchCommand(CommandArguments commandArguments, String indexName) {
2433      return isRoundRobinSearchCommand() ? commandArguments.add(indexName) : commandArguments.key(indexName);
2434    }
2435    private CommandArguments checkAndRoundRobinSearchCommand(CommandArguments commandArguments, byte[] indexName) {
2436      return isRoundRobinSearchCommand() ? commandArguments.add(indexName) : commandArguments.key(indexName);
2437    }
2438    private <T> CommandObject<T> directSearchCommand(CommandObject<T> object, String indexName) {
2439      object.getArguments().processKey(indexName);
2440      return object;
2441    }
2442    public final CommandObject<String> ftCreate(String indexName, IndexOptions indexOptions, Schema schema) {
2443      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(SearchCommand.CREATE).add(indexName)
2444          .addParams(indexOptions).add(SearchKeyword.SCHEMA);
2445      schema.fields.forEach(field -> args.addParams(field));
2446      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STRING);
2447    }

3113    public final CommandObject<String> cmsMerge(String destKey, Map<String, Long> keysAndWeights) {
3114      CommandArguments args = commandArguments(CountMinSketchCommand.MERGE).key(destKey);
3115      args.add(keysAndWeights.size());
3116      keysAndWeights.entrySet().forEach(entry -> args.key(entry.getKey()));
3117      args.add(RedisBloomKeyword.WEIGHTS);
3118      keysAndWeights.entrySet().forEach(entry -> args.add(entry.getValue()));
3119      return new CommandObject<>(args, BuilderFactory.STRING);
3120    }

3226    private JsonObjectMapper getJsonObjectMapper() {
3227      JsonObjectMapper localRef = this.jsonObjectMapper;
3228      if (Objects.isNull(localRef)) {
3229        synchronized (this) {
3230          localRef = this.jsonObjectMapper;
3231          if (Objects.isNull(localRef)) {
3232            this.jsonObjectMapper = localRef = new DefaultGsonObjectMapper();
3233          }
3234        }
3235      }
3236      return localRef;
3237    }

3257    private class JsonObjectBuilder<T> extends Builder<T> {
3258      private final Class<T> clazz;
3259      public JsonObjectBuilder(Class<T> clazz) {
3260        this.clazz = clazz;
3261      }
3262      @Override
3263      public T build(Object data) {
3264        return getJsonObjectMapper().fromJson(BuilderFactory.STRING.build(data), clazz);
3265      }
3266    }
3267    private class JsonObjectListBuilder<T> extends Builder<List<T>> {
3268      private final Class<T> clazz;
3269      public JsonObjectListBuilder(Class<T> clazz) {
3270        this.clazz = clazz;
3271      }
3272      @Override
3273      public List<T> build(Object data) {
3274        if (data == null) {
3275          return null;
3276        }
3277        List<String> list = BuilderFactory.STRING_LIST.build(data);
3278        return list.stream().map(s -> getJsonObjectMapper().fromJson(s, clazz)).collect(Collectors.toList());
3279      }
3280    }

3326    private CommandArguments addGeoCoordinateFlatMapArgs(CommandArguments args, Map<?, GeoCoordinate> map) {
3327      for (Map.Entry<? extends Object, GeoCoordinate> entry : map.entrySet()) {
3328        GeoCoordinate ord = entry.getValue();
3329        args.add(ord.getLongitude());
